        <div class="content">
         <header>
          <h3 class="article-name">
           Bored chimps at Czech zoos video chat during lockdown
          </h3>
          <p class="byline">
           <span class="by-author">
            By
            <span style="white-space:nowrap">
             Harry Baker
            </span>
           </span>
           <time class="published-date relative-date" data-published-date="2021-03-19T17:35:23Z" datetime="2021-03-19T17:35:23Z">
           </time>
          </p>
         </header>
         <p class="synopsis">
          Zookeepers from two zoos in the Czech Republic have set up big screens to allow their chimps to interact with each other via a video call.
         </p>
        </div>
       </article>
      </a>

           <h3 class="article-name">
            Alligators in Oklahoma turn into 'popsicles' sticking out of the frozen water
           </h3>
           <p class="byline">
            <span class="by-author">

             </span>

          <p class="synopsis">
           Alligators often 'snorkel' during cold snaps, so they don't become trapped underwater without access to air.
          </p>
